CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS gpuApi_products(
   id               INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,Name             VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL
  ,Architecture     VARCHAR(31) NOT NULL
  ,Boost_Clock      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Core_Speed       INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Memory           INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Memory_Speed     VARCHAR(8) NOT NULL
  ,Memory_Bandwidth VARCHAR(11)
  ,DVI_Connection   INTEGER 
  ,Dedicated        VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL
  ,Direct_X         VARCHAR(7) NOT NULL
  ,HDMI_Connection  INTEGER 
  ,Integrated       VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL
  ,L2_Cache         VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL
  ,Manufacturer     VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL
  ,Max_Power        VARCHAR(9)
  ,Memory_Bus       VARCHAR(8)
  ,Memory_Type      VARCHAR(6)
  ,Power_Connector  VARCHAR(20)
  ,Process          VARCHAR(4) NOT NULL
  ,Resolution_WxH   VARCHAR(9) NOT NULL
  ,SLI_Crossfire    VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL
);
